< text>
With many available storage options out there, we decided on this location as they have either met or exceeded all areas of criteria we were looking for in a Storage company.....Security, cleanliness and most importantly customer service support.

Upon meeting Nicole her personality was bubbly and inviting. Nicole was able to help us with information in deciding which storage size was perfect for our needs and even went as far as to walk and tour each unit so we could have a visual idea of the space offered. Mind you it's a pretty huge lot and each unit offered was not in the same building location so kudos to her for her patience and willingness! Each unit shown was clean and undamaged. Hallways leading to units had good ample amounts of lighting, great access to elevator lifts/stairways and had security cameras that kept watch.

When it came to pricing Nicole made everything pleasant as can be. She was able to quote us a price that was cheaper than what we initially reserved online and for a much bigger unit! All in all our experience with Nicole and public storage has been an extremely exceptional one and would recommend to anyone.</text>

<Rating>1</Rating>< review>
A rating of one star is actually being generous.  I am so upset right now.  Public Storage units are not cheap.  I had one of the smallest ones, and paid $150 a month for it.  For a long time.  Which is insane but that's another story.  I finally decided to evacuate, and to my dismay, my unit had a rat and roach infestation.  It was the grossest thing I have ever seen.  All my furniture was scratched and torn up by rats I'm assuming and there were rat droppings everywhere.  I also saw roaches in the unit.  I had planned to donate my stuff to Salvation Army but when I saw the condition of it, I knew they wouldn't accept it and frankly, I would be ashamed to try to even donate it so I cancelled the pickup.  I spoke with the district manager, and told her that I needed for the unit to be cleared out and that I didn't feel I should have to pay for it.  In my opinion it was unsafe to even enter the unit!  It smelled so bad!  She did NOT agree, and I thought that I was being extremely reasonable in not asking for a refund for all the months that I had paid for what has turned out to be a rat and roach motel!  I am so mad.  The worst part is, it seems that this is just a normal part of doing business for them.  Like it wasn't a big deal or surprising that they had a rat infestation.  Be warned, they apparently do not do anything to safeguard against rats or roaches, and they HAVE to know that they have a rat problem.  Before I even opened my unit, I could smell it!  I have never had such a horrible experience with any company.  All of my stuff is ruined because of their negligence, and they have the nerve to ask me to pay to clear it out when it's in such a state that I would rather DIEE than go in there.  Honestly it was so gross, I feel they shouldn't even WANT me to clear it out because I could be attacked by a rat/whatever other animals are residing in there, and that could lead to a lawsuit.  But they probably have some shady way to get out of that too - I tried talking to someone else, and she was like "well, your contract says you are storing at your own risk".  I am not taking this sitting down and they are going to wish they paid for me to clear it out.< /review>

<Review>Small fitness studio with guided group classes/workouts, boot camp-style. Depending on time of day, you can get from a few people to a crowded room (I believe 24 is the max, which is a lot of people for its small space).

Coaches are friendly and the heart rate monitor workout helps you keep track of your goals and target. I feel that sometimes some of the coaches try to push people to go farther/faster/heavier than they should, but of course you're not forced into it.

Nice premium fitness studio, not for the light of wallet. Similar concept/style in many ways to Barry's Fitness (which is literally across the street from them); except, I like the space at Orangetheory better, because you can see outdoors and it's not a dark, enclosed windowless tunnel like the Barry's across the street.

Overall a really good workout with good facilities and friendly coaches. Really needs more bathrooms/showers (they only have 2 each), but they literally have no more space.< /Review>< pics>

<Review>I am posting negatively about a business for the first time ever. If I ever take the time to post it is usually for great customer service, or satisfaction.

Today I showed up at the royal oaks post office to have my passport reinstated. The time states that you can do this up until 6:30 in the post office, office. Mind you I understand I need to be there before that to actually get it taken care of. I got there at 6:15, and the doors were locked. There was an Asian man, not calling him a gentleman, behind the desk, right by the closed doors. I tried to open them three times and he didn't look up. I politely knocked, and no look. I decided to try to open the doors harder, maybe I was just mistaken by how the door opens? Nope, they were locked and the Asian man finally decided to glance up for two seconds to give me a disgusted look and point to the other double doors on the side of the building. He must've thought I was there to drop off mail.  I figured maybe as it nears closing time they only have those doors open. I go to the other doors and they are locked as well, but now he's far enough away to where him ignoring me does not seem unreasonable. I took advantage of the mail delivery window with the doorbell next to me, and used that to finally have an employee there speak with me. They started by abruptly saying it closes at 6 (I was now in the area of the post office that does), and the time was now around 6:18-6:20. I said I was there for my passport and that the office was closed and he was not paying attention to me. They fired back saying it takes about 20 minutes so they wouldn't be able to help. I was frustrated, so I do admit I snapped a bit and said that I was in the correct spot earlier but he didn't open the door or pay me any notice. Their last excuse was that he was having a bad day?! I ended up exclaiming that I just did not want my time to be wasted at this point and would appreciate them telling me if I at least have the correct paper work and documentation so that I could come back and take care of it. As this happened, i saw the Asian man walk back to the office to pretty much hide, I asked if i could talk to him about that to be sure, and the lady said she could help me as she does passports too. No answering machine, no answer, nothing.

Then I try the two other numbers I can find for this same post office (one is the number caller ID lists the call came from). Same thing.

Finally, on my fifth call to the first number, someone picks up after 32 rings. And then promptly says "goddamn" and hangs up the phone on me before I can say anything.

They call me back the next day again, and rudely tell me "you were really hard to get ahold of." Really? Try answering your phone.
